## 2. Sylva CLI for Debugging (`tools/debug_cli.sv`)

A command‑line interface to control recording, breakpoints, and replay.

```sylva
// tools/debug_cli.sv – Command line interface for the Polyglot Debugger
module polyglot::tools::debug_cli

use polyglot::debugger::PolyglotDebugger
use core::io::{println, read_line}
use core::string::String

let debugger = PolyglotDebugger::connect("aether://debugger")

pub fn main(args: List<String>) {
    if args.is_empty() {
        println("Usage: debug <record|stop|list|replay|breakpoint|query|resume> [options]")
        return
    }
    match args[0] {
        "record" => cmd_record(args.tail())
        "stop" => cmd_stop(args.tail())
        "list" => cmd_list()
        "replay" => cmd_replay(args.tail())
        "breakpoint" => cmd_breakpoint(args.tail())
        "query" => cmd_query(args.tail())
        "resume" => cmd_resume(args.tail())
        _ => println("Unknown command")
    }
}

fn cmd_record(args: List<String>) {
    let name = args.get(0).unwrap_or("trace_" + now())
    let id = debugger.start_recording(name)
    println("Recording started. Session ID: " + id)
    println("Use 'debug stop <id>' to finish.")
}

fn cmd_stop(args: List<String>) {
    let id = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    if id.is_empty() {
        println("Usage: debug stop <session_id>")
        return
    }
    match debugger.stop_recording(id) {
        Ok(stored) => println("Recording saved: " + stored.id)
        Err(e) => println("Error: " + e)
    }
}

fn cmd_list() {
    let recordings = debugger.list_recordings()
    if recordings.is_empty() {
        println("No recordings found.")
        return
    }
    println("Recordings:")
    for rec in recordings {
        println(format!("  {} | {} | {} events | {}", rec.id, rec.name, rec.event_count, rec.timestamp))
    }
}

fn cmd_replay(args: List<String>) {
    let id = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    if id.is_empty() {
        println("Usage: debug replay <session_id>")
        return
    }
    match debugger.replay(id) {
        Ok(result) => if result.success {
            println("Replay succeeded. All events matched.")
        } else {
            println("Replay failed. Divergence detected.")
        }
        Err(e) => println("Error: " + e)
    }
}

fn cmd_breakpoint(args: List<String>) {
    let subcmd = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    match subcmd {
        "set" => {
            let src = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            let tgt = args.get(2).unwrap_or("")
            let func = args.get(3).unwrap_or("")
            let id = debugger.set_breakpoint(src, tgt, func)
            println("Breakpoint set. ID: " + id)
        }
        "remove" => {
            let id = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            let success = debugger.remove_breakpoint(id)
            println(if success { "Breakpoint removed" } else { "Breakpoint not found" })
        }
        "list" => {
            let bps = debugger.list_breakpoints()
            for bp in bps {
                println(format!("{}: {}→{} {} (hit {})", bp.id, bp.condition.source_lang, bp.condition.target_lang, bp.condition.function, bp.hit_count))
            }
        }
        _ => println("Usage: debug breakpoint set|remove|list")
    }
}

fn cmd_query(args: List<String>) {
    let src = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    let tgt = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
    let events = debugger.query_traces(src, tgt)
    for ev in events {
        println(format!("{}: {}.{}() -> {:.3}ms", ev.timestamp, ev.module, ev.function, ev.duration_us / 1000.0))
    }
}

fn cmd_resume(args: List<String>) {
    let id = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    if id.is_empty() {
        println("Usage: debug resume <session_id>")
        return
    }
    match debugger.resume(id) {
        Ok(()) => println("Session resumed")
        Err(e) => println("Error: " + e)
    }
}
```

---

## 3. Web UI for Debugging (`debug_ui/index.html`)

A simple web interface to view recordings, set breakpoints, and replay traces.

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <title>Polyglot Debugger</title>
    <style>
        body { font-family: system-ui, sans-serif; background: #0f172a; color: #e2e8f0; margin: 0; padding: 2rem; }
        h1 { margin-bottom: 1rem; }
        .flex { display: flex; gap: 1rem; margin-bottom: 1rem; flex-wrap: wrap; }
        button, select, input { padding: 0.5rem 1rem; background: #1e293b; border: 1px solid #334155; border-radius: 8px; color: white; cursor: pointer; }
        button { background: #3b82f6; border: none; }
        button:hover { background: #2563eb; }
        table { width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; }
        th, td { text-align: left; padding: 0.5rem; border-bottom: 1px solid #334155; }
        .event-row { cursor: pointer; }
        .event-row:hover { background: #1e293b; }
        .breakpoint-panel { margin-top: 2rem; }
        .breakpoint-panel input { width: 120px; }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
<h1>🐞 Polyglot Debugger</h1>
<div class="flex">
    <button onclick="startRecording()">Start Recording</button>
    <button onclick="stopRecording()">Stop Recording</button>
    <button onclick="loadRecordings()">Refresh List</button>
    <button onclick="showBreakpointDialog()">Set Breakpoint</button>
</div>
<div>
    <h3>Recordings</h3>
    <table id="recordingsTable">
        <thead><tr><th>ID</th><th>Name</th><th>Events</th><th>Timestamp</th><th>Actions</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody></tbody>
    </table>
</div>
<div>
    <h3>Events (last recording)</h3>
    <table id="eventsTable">
        <thead><tr><th>Time</th><th>Source</th><th>Target</th><th>Function</th><th>Duration (µs)</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody></tbody>
    </table>
</div>
<div class="breakpoint-panel" id="breakpointPanel">
    <h3>Breakpoints</h3>
    <ul id="breakpointsList"></ul>
</div>

<script>
    const ws = new WebSocket("ws://localhost:8094");
    ws.onmessage = (e) => {
        const msg = JSON.parse(e.data);
        if (msg.event === "session_status") updateSessionStatus(msg.session);
        else if (msg.event === "recording_list") displayRecordings(msg.recordings);
        else if (msg.event === "breakpoint_hit") alert(`Breakpoint hit: ${msg.src} → ${msg.tgt} :: ${msg.func}`);
    };

    function startRecording() {
        const name = prompt("Recording name:", "trace_" + Date.now());
        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ command: "start_recording", name }));
    }
    function stopRecording() {
        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ command: "stop_recording", session_id: currentSessionId }));
    }
    function loadRecordings() {
        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ command: "list_recordings" }));
    }
    function showBreakpointDialog() {
        const src = prompt("Source language (or empty for any):", "");
        const tgt = prompt("Target language (or empty for any):", "");
        const func = prompt("Function name (or empty for any):", "");
        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ command: "set_breakpoint", condition: { source_lang: src || null, target_lang: tgt || null, function: func || null } }));
    }
    function loadBreakpoints() {
        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ command: "list_breakpoints" }));
    }
    function displayRecordings(recordings) {
        const tbody = document.querySelector("#recordingsTable tbody");
        tbody.innerHTML = "";
        for (const rec of recordings) {
            const row = tbody.insertRow();
            row.insertCell(0).innerText = rec.id;
            row.insertCell(1).innerText = rec.name;
            row.insertCell(2).innerText = rec.event_count;
            row.insertCell(3).innerText = new Date(rec.timestamp).toLocaleString();
            const actions = row.insertCell(4);
            const replayBtn = document.createElement("button");
            replayBtn.innerText = "Replay";
            replayBtn.onclick = () => ws.send(JSON.stringify({ command: "replay", session_id: rec.id }));
            actions.appendChild(replayBtn);
        }
    }
    function updateSessionStatus(session) {
        currentSessionId = session.id;
        const events = session.events || [];
        const tbody = document.querySelector("#eventsTable tbody");
        tbody.innerHTML = "";
        for (const ev of events) {
            const row = tbody.insertRow();
            row.insertCell(0).innerText = ev.started_at;
            row.insertCell(1).innerText = ev.source;
            row.insertCell(2).innerText = ev.target;
            row.insertCell(3).innerText = ev.function;
            row.insertCell(4).innerText = ev.duration_us;
        }
    }
    loadRecordings();
    setInterval(loadRecordings, 5000);
</script>
</body>
</html>
```

---

## 4. Integration with Existing Components

The debugger integrates with the Connections Router (already instrumented), the Security Manager (to check permissions for recording sensitive calls), and the Workflow Orchestrator (to record workflow steps). Add to the deployment script:

```bash
echo "[5] Starting Polyglot Debugger..."
aether run services/debugger.ae --name debugger --router router --security security-mgr --store trace-store --ws-port 8094
echo "Debugger UI available at http://localhost:8095"
```

---

## 5. Example Use Case

```bash
# Record a session
debug record "my_session"
# Run some polyglot workflow
wf submit examples/workflows/ci_pipeline.yaml
# Stop recording
debug stop <session_id>
# List recordings
debug list
# Replay the session
debug replay <session_id>
```

The recorded trace is deterministic; replaying it will produce identical results. If a bug occurred during the original run, replay will reproduce it exactly.

---

## 6. Conclusion

The Polyglot Debugging & Tracing Service completes the Omnisystem's polyglot tooling. Developers can now:

- Record cross‑language call sequences
- Replay them deterministically
- Set breakpoints on any language pair or function
- Query traces by source, target, or duration
- Integrate with the CI pipeline to catch regressions

Together with the Package Manager, Security Manager, and Workflow Orchestrator, the Omnisystem now provides a full lifecycle for polyglot development: discover, install, secure, orchestrate, and debug – all across 750+ languages. 🚀", "```aether
// services/ci_orchestrator.ae – Polyglot CI/CD Orchestration Engine
// Automatically tests all language connectors on every commit, manages canary
// deployments, detects regressions, and coordinates the full validation pipeline.

actor PolyglotCIOrchestrator {
    var router: ConnectionsRouter
    var index: IndexService
    var packages: PolyglotPackageManager
    var security: PolyglotSecurityManager
    var workflow: WorkflowOrchestrator
    var debugger: PolyglotDebugger
    var uvm: UvmRunner
    var perf: PerformanceAnalyzer

    var pipelines: Map<String, PipelineState> = empty()
    var canaries: Map<String, CanaryDeployment> = empty()
    var baselines: Map<String, BaselineSnapshot> = empty()
    var webhook_registry: Map<String, WebhookConfig> = empty()
    var websocket: WebSocketServer

    var max_parallel_pipelines: u32 = 10
    var active_pipelines: u32 = 0

    on new(
        router_addr: String, index_addr: String, packages_addr: String,
        security_addr: String, workflow_addr: String, debugger_addr: String,
        uvm_addr: String, perf_addr: String, ws_port: u16
    ) {
        router = ConnectionsRouter::connect(router_addr)
        index = IndexService::connect(index_addr)
        packages = PolyglotPackageManager::connect(packages_addr)
        security = PolyglotSecurityManager::connect(security_addr)
        workflow = WorkflowOrchestrator::connect(workflow_addr)
        debugger = PolyglotDebugger::connect(debugger_addr)
        uvm = UvmRunner::connect(uvm_addr)
        perf = PerformanceAnalyzer::connect(perf_addr)
        websocket = WebSocketServer::bind(ws_port)
        load_baselines()
        start_api()
        start_pipeline_scheduler()
    }

    // ── Pipeline Management ────────────────────────────────────────────

    on trigger_pipeline(trigger: PipelineTrigger) -> String {
        let id = generate_pipeline_id()
        let pipeline = PipelineState {
            id: id.clone(),
            trigger,
            status: PipelineStatus::Queued,
            stages: build_stage_plan(trigger),
            current_stage: 0,
            started_at: None,
            completed_at: None,
            results: Map::new(),
            artifacts: Map::new(),
        }
        pipelines.set(id.clone(), pipeline)
        broadcast_pipeline_update(id)
        id
    }

    fn build_stage_plan(trigger: PipelineTrigger) -> List<PipelineStage> {
        let mut stages = Vec::new()

        // Stage 1: Lint & Static Analysis (all changed packages)
        stages.push(PipelineStage {
            name: "lint",
            description: "Lint and static analysis across all changed language modules",
            timeout_secs: 300,
            retry_count: 1,
            optional: false,
            steps: trigger.changed_packages.map(|pkg| PipelineStep {
                package: pkg,
                action: "lint",
                language: packages.get_language(pkg).unwrap_or("titan"),
            }),
        })

        // Stage 2: Unit Tests (per language)
        stages.push(PipelineStage {
            name: "unit_tests",
            description: "Run language‑specific unit tests for each changed module",
            timeout_secs: 600,
            retry_count: 2,
            optional: false,
            steps: trigger.changed_packages.map(|pkg| PipelineStep {
                package: pkg,
                action: "test",
                language: packages.get_language(pkg).unwrap_or("titan"),
            }),
        })

        // Stage 3: Cross‑Language Integration Tests (full matrix for changed pairs)
        let affected_pairs = compute_affected_pairs(trigger.changed_packages)
        stages.push(PipelineStage {
            name: "cross_lang_tests",
            description: format!("Run UVM tests for {} affected language pairs", affected_pairs.len()),
            timeout_secs: 1800,
            retry_count: 1,
            optional: false,
            steps: affected_pairs.map(|(src, tgt)| PipelineStep {
                package: format!("{}->{}", src, tgt),
                action: "cross_test",
                language: src,
            }),
        })

        // Stage 4: Performance Regression Check
        stages.push(PipelineStage {
            name: "perf_regression",
            description: "Compare connector performance against baseline",
            timeout_secs: 900,
            retry_count: 0,
            optional: trigger.is_pr,  // optional for PRs, required for main
            steps: affected_pairs.map(|(src, tgt)| PipelineStep {
                package: format!("{}->{}", src, tgt),
                action: "perf_check",
                language: src,
            }),
        })

        // Stage 5: Canary Deployment (main branch only)
        if !trigger.is_pr {
            stages.push(PipelineStage {
                name: "canary_deploy",
                description: "Gradually roll out updated connectors to production",
                timeout_secs: 3600,
                retry_count: 0,
                optional: false,
                steps: trigger.changed_packages.map(|pkg| PipelineStep {
                    package: pkg,
                    action: "canary",
                    language: packages.get_language(pkg).unwrap_or("titan"),
                }),
            })
        }

        stages
    }

    fn compute_affected_pairs(changed_packages: List<String>) -> List<(String, String)> {
        // Determine which language pairs are affected by the changed packages
        let mut pairs = Set::new()
        for pkg in changed_packages {
            let lang = packages.get_language(pkg).unwrap_or("unknown")
            // This language is a source – find all targets it connects to
            let entries = index.list_by_source(lang)
            for entry in entries {
                pairs.add((lang.clone(), entry.target_lang))
            }
            // This language is a target – find all sources that connect to it
            let entries = index.list_by_target(lang)
            for entry in entries {
                pairs.add((entry.source_lang, lang.clone()))
            }
        }
        pairs.to_list()
    }

    // ── Pipeline Execution ──────────────────────────────────────────────

    fn start_pipeline_scheduler() {
        loop {
            sleep_ms(5000)
            while active_pipelines < max_parallel_pipelines {
                let next = pipelines.values()
                    .filter(|p| p.status == PipelineStatus::Queued)
                    .sorted_by(|a, b| a.trigger.priority - b.trigger.priority)
                    .first()
                if next == null { break }
                active_pipelines += 1
                spawn_execute_pipeline(next.id)
            }
        }
    }

    async fn execute_pipeline(id: String) {
        let mut pipeline = pipelines.get_mut(id).ok_or_else(|| "Pipeline not found".to_string())?;
        pipeline.status = PipelineStatus::Running
        pipeline.started_at = Some(now())
        broadcast_pipeline_update(id)

        for (stage_idx, stage) in pipeline.stages.iter().enumerate() {
            pipeline.current_stage = stage_idx
            broadcast_pipeline_update(id)

            let mut stage_result = StageResult {
                name: stage.name,
                passed: 0,
                failed: 0,
                skipped: 0,
                duration_secs: 0,
            }
            let stage_start = now()

            // Execute steps in parallel within the stage
            let semaphore = Semaphore::new(max_parallel_pipelines)
            let mut futures = Vec::new()

            for step in stage.steps {
                let sem = semaphore.clone()
                let step_clone = step.clone()
                futures.push(async {
                    let _permit = sem.acquire().await
                    execute_pipeline_step(id, step_clone, stage.retry_count, stage.timeout_secs).await
                })
            }

            for future in futures {
                let result = future.await
                match result {
                    StepOutcome::Passed => stage_result.passed += 1
                    StepOutcome::Failed => stage_result.failed += 1
                    StepOutcome::Skipped => stage_result.skipped += 1
                }
            }

            stage_result.duration_secs = (now() - stage_start) / 1000
            pipeline.results.set(stage.name, stage_result)

            // If stage is required and any step failed, fail the pipeline
            if !stage.optional && stage_result.failed > 0 {
                pipeline.status = PipelineStatus::Failed
                pipeline.completed_at = Some(now())
                broadcast_pipeline_update(id)
                return
            }
        }

        pipeline.status = PipelineStatus::Passed
        pipeline.completed_at = Some(now())
        // Update baselines for next comparison
        update_baselines(pipeline.trigger.changed_packages)
        broadcast_pipeline_update(id)
        active_pipelines -= 1
    }

    async fn execute_pipeline_step(
        pipeline_id: String, step: PipelineStep,
        retry_count: u32, timeout_secs: u64,
    ) -> StepOutcome {
        let mut attempts = 0
        while attempts <= retry_count {
            match step.action {
                "lint" => {
                    let result = run_lint(step.package, step.language, timeout_secs).await
                    if result.is_ok() { return StepOutcome::Passed }
                }
                "test" => {
                    let result = run_unit_tests(step.package, step.language, timeout_secs).await
                    if result.is_ok() { return StepOutcome::Passed }
                }
                "cross_test" => {
                    let parts = step.package.split("->").collect()
                    let src = parts[0]
                    let tgt = parts[1]
                    let result = run_cross_test(src, tgt, timeout_secs).await
                    if result.is_ok() { return StepOutcome::Passed }
                }
                "perf_check" => {
                    let parts = step.package.split("->").collect()
                    let src = parts[0]
                    let tgt = parts[1]
                    let result = check_performance_regression(src, tgt).await
                    if result.is_ok() { return StepOutcome::Passed }
                }
                "canary" => {
                    let result = deploy_canary(step.package, step.language).await
                    if result.is_ok() { return StepOutcome::Passed }
                }
                _ => return StepOutcome::Skipped
            }
            attempts += 1
        }
        StepOutcome::Failed
    }

    // ── Canary Deployments ─────────────────────────────────────────────

    async fn deploy_canary(package: String, language: String) -> Result<(), String> {
        let canary_id = generate_canary_id()
        let deployment = CanaryDeployment {
            id: canary_id.clone(),
            package: package.clone(),
            language: language.clone(),
            target_percentage: 5,  // start at 5% of nodes
            current_percentage: 0,
            status: CanaryStatus::Initializing,
            metrics: CanaryMetrics::default(),
            started_at: now(),
        }
        canaries.set(canary_id.clone(), deployment)

        // Phase 1: Deploy to 5% of nodes
        update_canary_percentage(canary_id, 5).await?;
        sleep_ms(300_000)  // observe for 5 minutes

        if !canary_health_check(canary_id).await {
            rollback_canary(canary_id).await?;
            return Err("Canary health check failed at 5%".to_string())
        }

        // Phase 2: Deploy to 25% of nodes
        update_canary_percentage(canary_id, 25).await?;
        sleep_ms(600_000)  // observe for 10 minutes

        if !canary_health_check(canary_id).await {
            rollback_canary(canary_id).await?;
            return Err("Canary health check failed at 25%".to_string())
        }

        // Phase 3: Deploy to 100% of nodes
        update_canary_percentage(canary_id, 100).await?;
        sleep_ms(300_000)  // final observation

        if !canary_health_check(canary_id).await {
            rollback_canary(canary_id).await?;
            return Err("Canary health check failed at 100%".to_string())
        }

        canaries.get_mut(canary_id).unwrap().status = CanaryStatus::Completed
        Ok(())
    }

    async fn update_canary_percentage(canary_id: String, percentage: u32) -> Result<(), String> {
        let mut canary = canaries.get_mut(canary_id).ok_or("Canary not found")?;
        canary.current_percentage = percentage
        // Actually deploy to the target percentage of nodes via UMS distribution
        let package_hash = index.resolve(canary.language, "titan", "latest", "latest")?.connector_hash
        ums::distribute_with_percentage(package_hash, percentage).await?;
        Ok(())
    }

    async fn canary_health_check(canary_id: String) -> bool {
        let canary = canaries.get(canary_id).unwrap()
        let stats = perf.get_stats(canary.language, "titan")
        if stats == null { return true }

        // Check that error rate hasn't spiked
        let error_rate = if stats.total_calls > 0 {
            (stats.total_calls - stats.success_calls) as f32 / stats.total_calls as f32
        } else { 0.0 }

        if error_rate > 0.01 { return false }  // >1% error rate

        // Check that latency hasn't degraded significantly
        let baseline = baselines.get(format!("{}:{}", canary.language, canary.package))
        if baseline != null {
            let current_avg = stats.total_latency_us / stats.total_calls
            if current_avg > baseline.avg_latency_us * 2 { return false }
        }

        true
    }

    async fn rollback_canary(canary_id: String) -> Result<(), String> {
        let canary = canaries.get_mut(canary_id).ok_or("Canary not found")?;
        canary.status = CanaryStatus::RolledBack
        // Revert to previous version via UMS
        ums::rollback_to_previous(canary.package).await?;
        Ok(())
    }

    // ── Baseline Management ────────────────────────────────────────────

    fn load_baselines() {
        let stored = ums::get_module("polyglot_baselines_latest")
        if stored != null {
            baselines = deserialize(stored)
        }
    }

    fn update_baselines(packages: List<String>) {
        for pkg in packages {
            let lang = packages.get_language(pkg).unwrap_or("unknown")
            let stats = perf.get_stats(lang, "titan")
            if stats != null && stats.total_calls > 100 {
                baselines.set(format!("{}:{}", lang, pkg), BaselineSnapshot {
                    avg_latency_us: stats.total_latency_us / stats.total_calls,
                    success_rate: stats.success_calls as f32 / stats.total_calls as f32,
                    total_calls: stats.total_calls,
                    recorded_at: now(),
                })
            }
        }
        // Persist baselines
        ums::put("polyglot_baselines_latest", serialize(baselines))
    }

    async fn check_performance_regression(src: String, tgt: String) -> Result<(), String> {
        let stats = perf.get_stats(src, tgt)
        if stats == null { return Ok(()) }

        let baseline = baselines.get(format!("{}:{}", src, tgt))
        if baseline == null { return Ok(()) }

        let current_avg = stats.total_latency_us / stats.total_calls
        let regression_threshold = baseline.avg_latency_us * 1.1  // 10% degradation threshold

        if current_avg > regression_threshold && stats.total_calls > 1000 {
            return Err(format!(
                "Performance regression: {}µs → {}µs (baseline: {}µs, threshold: {}µs)",
                baseline.avg_latency_us, current_avg, baseline.avg_latency_us, regression_threshold
            ))
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    // ── Webhook Integration ────────────────────────────────────────────

    on register_webhook(config: WebhookConfig) -> String {
        let id = generate_webhook_id()
        webhook_registry.set(id.clone(), config)
        id
    }

    on handle_webhook(payload: WebhookPayload) -> Result<String, String> {
        let config = webhook_registry.get(payload.source)
        if config == null { return Err("Unknown webhook source") }

        // Verify webhook signature
        if !verify_webhook_signature(payload, config.secret) {
            return Err("Invalid webhook signature")
        }

        // Determine changed packages from the payload
        let changed_packages = extract_changed_packages(payload, config)

        let trigger = PipelineTrigger {
            changed_packages,
            is_pr: payload.event == "pull_request",
            priority: if payload.event == "push" && payload.branch == "main" { 10 } else { 5 },
        }

        let pipeline_id = trigger_pipeline(trigger)
        Ok(pipeline_id)
    }

    // ── WebSocket API ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

    fn start_api() {
        websocket.on_message(|msg| {
            match msg.command {
                "trigger" => {
                    let id = trigger_pipeline(msg.trigger)
                    websocket.reply(json({ pipeline_id: id }))
                }
                "status" => {
                    let pipeline = pipelines.get(msg.pipeline_id)
                    websocket.reply(pipeline)
                }
                "list" => {
                    let all = pipelines.values().map(|p| PipelineSummary {
                        id: p.id, status: p.status,
                        progress: p.current_stage as f32 / p.stages.len() as f32,
                        passed: p.results.values().map(|r| r.passed).sum(),
                        failed: p.results.values().map(|r| r.failed).sum(),
                    })
                    websocket.reply(all)
                }
                "canary_status" => {
                    let status = canaries.get(msg.canary_id)
                    websocket.reply(status)
                }
                "baselines" => {
                    websocket.reply(baselines)
                }
                "register_webhook" => {
                    let id = register_webhook(msg.config)
                    websocket.reply(json({ webhook_id: id }))
                }
                _ => websocket.reply(error("Unknown command"))
            }
        })
    }

    fn broadcast_pipeline_update(id: String) {
        let pipeline = pipelines.get(id)
        if pipeline != null {
            websocket.broadcast(json({ event: "pipeline_update", pipeline }))
        }
    }
}

// ── Type Definitions ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

struct PipelineTrigger {
    changed_packages: List<String>,
    is_pr: bool,
    priority: u32,
}

struct PipelineState {
    id: String,
    trigger: PipelineTrigger,
    status: PipelineStatus,
    stages: List<PipelineStage>,
    current_stage: u32,
    started_at: Option<u64>,
    completed_at: Option<u64>,
    results: Map<String, StageResult>,
    artifacts: Map<String, String>,
}

enum PipelineStatus {
    Queued, Running, Passed, Failed, Cancelled,
}

struct PipelineStage {
    name: String,
    description: String,
    timeout_secs: u64,
    retry_count: u32,
    optional: bool,
    steps: List<PipelineStep>,
}

struct PipelineStep {
    package: String,
    action: String,
    language: String,
}

struct StageResult {
    name: String,
    passed: u32,
    failed: u32,
    skipped: u32,
    duration_secs: u64,
}

enum StepOutcome {
    Passed, Failed, Skipped,
}

struct PipelineSummary {
    id: String,
    status: PipelineStatus,
    progress: f32,
    passed: u32,
    failed: u32,
}

struct CanaryDeployment {
    id: String,
    package: String,
    language: String,
    target_percentage: u32,
    current_percentage: u32,
    status: CanaryStatus,
    metrics: CanaryMetrics,
    started_at: u64,
}

enum CanaryStatus {
    Initializing, Deploying, Observing, Completed, RolledBack,
}

struct CanaryMetrics {
    error_rate: f32,
    avg_latency_us: u64,
    p99_latency_us: u64,
    request_count: u64,
    nodes_affected: u32,
}

struct BaselineSnapshot {
    avg_latency_us: u64,
    success_rate: f32,
    total_calls: u64,
    recorded_at: u64,
}

struct WebhookConfig {
    source: String,
    secret: String,
    events: List<String>,
    package_mapping: Map<String, String>,
}

struct WebhookPayload {
    source: String,
    event: String,
    branch: String,
    changed_files: List<String>,
    signature: String,
}
```

```sylva
// tools/ci_cli.sv – CLI for the Polyglot CI/CD Orchestrator
module polyglot::tools::ci_cli

use polyglot::ci_orchestrator::PolyglotCIOrchestrator
use core::io::{println, read_file}
use core::string::String
use core::time::sleep_ms

let ci = PolyglotCIOrchestrator::connect("aether://ci-orchestrator")

pub fn main(args: List<String>) {
    if args.is_empty() {
        println("Usage: ci <trigger|status|list|canary|baselines|watch|webhook> [options]")
        return
    }
    match args[0] {
        "trigger" => cmd_trigger(args.tail())
        "status" => cmd_status(args.tail())
        "list" => cmd_list()
        "canary" => cmd_canary(args.tail())
        "baselines" => cmd_baselines()
        "watch" => cmd_watch(args.tail())
        "webhook" => cmd_webhook(args.tail())
        _ => println("Unknown command: " + args[0])
    }
}

fn cmd_trigger(args: List<String>) {
    let packages = args.filter(|a| !a.starts_with("--"))
    let is_pr = args.contains("--pr")
    let trigger = PipelineTrigger {
        changed_packages: packages,
        is_pr,
        priority: if args.contains("--priority") {
            args.get(args.index_of("--priority").unwrap() + 1).unwrap_or("5").parse_u32().unwrap_or(5)
        } else { 5 },
    }
    let id = ci.trigger_pipeline(trigger)
    println("Pipeline triggered: " + id)
    println("Monitor with: ci watch " + id)
}

fn cmd_status(args: List<String>) {
    let id = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    if id.is_empty() {
        println("Usage: ci status <pipeline_id>")
        return
    }
    let pipeline = ci.get_pipeline(id)
    match pipeline {
        Some(p) => {
            println(format!("Pipeline: {} | Status: {}", p.id, p.status))
            println(format!("Progress: {}/{} stages", p.current_stage + 1, p.stages.len()))
            println("Stage Results:")
            for (name, result) in p.results {
                let icon = if result.failed == 0 { "✅" } else { "❌" }
                println(format!("  {} {} | {} passed, {} failed, {} skipped | {}s",
                    icon, name, result.passed, result.failed, result.skipped, result.duration_secs))
            }
        }
        None => println("Pipeline not found")
    }
}

fn cmd_list() {
    let pipelines = ci.list_pipelines()
    if pipelines.is_empty() {
        println("No pipelines found.")
        return
    }
    println("Active Pipelines:")
    for p in pipelines {
        let icon = match p.status {
            PipelineStatus::Running => "🔄"
            PipelineStatus::Passed => "✅"
            PipelineStatus::Failed => "❌"
            PipelineStatus::Queued => "⏳"
            PipelineStatus::Cancelled => "⛔"
        }
        println(format!("  {} {} | {} | {:.0}% | {}/{}",
            icon, p.id, p.status, p.progress * 100, p.passed, p.passed + p.failed))
    }
}

fn cmd_canary(args: List<String>) {
    let subcmd = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    match subcmd {
        "status" => {
            let id = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            let status = ci.get_canary_status(id)
            match status {
                Some(s) => println(format!("Canary {}: {} | {}/{}% | Error rate: {:.2}%",
                    s.id, s.status, s.current_percentage, s.target_percentage, s.metrics.error_rate * 100)),
                None => println("Canary not found")
            }
        }
        "list" => {
            let canaries = ci.list_canaries()
            for c in canaries {
                println(format!("{} | {} | {}/{}% | {}",
                    c.id, c.status, c.current_percentage, c.target_percentage, c.package))
            }
        }
        _ => println("Usage: ci canary status|list")
    }
}

fn cmd_baselines() {
    let baselines = ci.get_baselines()
    if baselines.is_empty() {
        println("No baselines recorded.")
        return
    }
    println("Performance Baselines:")
    for (key, baseline) in baselines {
        println(format!("  {} | {}µs avg | {:.1}% success | {} calls",
            key, baseline.avg_latency_us, baseline.success_rate * 100, baseline.total_calls))
    }
}

fn cmd_watch(args: List<String>) {
    let id = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    if id.is_empty() {
        println("Usage: ci watch <pipeline_id>")
        return
    }
    println("Watching pipeline " + id + " (Ctrl+C to stop)...")
    loop {
        let pipeline = ci.get_pipeline(id)
        match pipeline {
            Some(p) => {
                let progress = if p.stages.is_empty() { 0.0 } else {
                    p.current_stage as f32 / p.stages.len() as f32
                }
                println(format!("\r  Status: {} | Stage {}/{} | {:.0}%",
                    p.status, p.current_stage + 1, p.stages.len(), progress * 100))
                if p.status == PipelineStatus::Passed || p.status == PipelineStatus::Failed {
                    println("")
                    cmd_status([id])
                    break
                }
            }
            None => {
                println("Pipeline not found")
                break
            }
        }
        sleep_ms(2000)
    }
}

fn cmd_webhook(args: List<String>) {
    let subcmd = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    match subcmd {
        "register" => {
            let source = args.get(1).unwrap_or("github")
            let secret = args.get(2).unwrap_or("")
            let config = WebhookConfig {
                source,
                secret,
                events: ["push", "pull_request"],
                package_mapping: Map::new(),
            }
            let id = ci.register_webhook(config)
            println("Webhook registered: " + id)
        }
        "list" => {
            let hooks = ci.list_webhooks()
            for hook in hooks {
                println(format!("{} | {} | {}", hook.id, hook.source, hook.events.join(", ")))
            }
        }
        _ => println("Usage: ci webhook register|list")
    }
}
```

The Polyglot CI/CD Orchestrator completes the Omnisystem Polyglot Core's operational infrastructure. With automated linting, unit tests, cross‑language integration tests, performance regression detection, canary deployments, and webhook integration, the entire polyglot ecosystem now benefits from continuous validation and safe, gradual rollouts. Every language connector is automatically tested, benchmarked, and deployed with zero‑downtime canary strategies—ensuring the 750+ language fabric remains reliable, performant, and production‑ready at all times.", "# Omnisystem Polyglot Core – Next Segment: Polyglot Resource Scheduler & Autoscaler

This deliverable provides the **complete, production‑grade code** for the **Polyglot Resource Scheduler & Autoscaler** – a system that dynamically allocates CPU, memory, and I/O quotas to language runtimes based on workload, enforces global resource limits, and automatically scales connector pools up or down. It integrates with the Performance Analyzer (for load metrics), Security Manager (for capability quotas), and CI/CD Orchestrator (for deployment‑driven scaling). All components are in Aether, Titan, and Sylva.

---

## 1. Polyglot Resource Scheduler (`services/resource_scheduler.ae`)

This Aether actor manages resource allocations for all language runtimes, monitors system capacity, and makes scheduling decisions.

```aether
// services/resource_scheduler.ae – Resource Scheduler & Autoscaler
actor PolyglotResourceScheduler {
    var perf: PerformanceAnalyzer
    var security: PolyglotSecurityManager
    var router: ConnectionsRouter
    var quotas: Map<String, RuntimeQuota> = empty()   // language -> quota
    var node_capacity: NodeCapacity
    var scaling_policies: List<ScalingPolicy> = empty()
    var scaling_history: List<ScalingEvent> = empty()
    var websocket: WebSocketServer

    on new(perf_addr: String, security_addr: String, router_addr: String, ws_port: u16) {
        perf = PerformanceAnalyzer::connect(perf_addr)
        security = PolyglotSecurityManager::connect(security_addr)
        router = ConnectionsRouter::connect(router_addr)
        websocket = WebSocketServer::bind(ws_port)
        load_node_capacity()
        load_quotas()
        start_scheduler_loop()
        start_scaler_loop()
    }

    // ── Quota Management ───────────────────────────────────────────────

    on set_quota(language: String, quota: RuntimeQuota) -> Result<(), String> {
        if !validate_quota(quota) { return Err("Invalid quota (exceeds node capacity)") }
        quotas.set(language, quota)
        apply_quota(language, quota)
        audit_log::log("quota_set", language, quota)
        Ok(())
    }

    on get_quota(language: String) -> Option<RuntimeQuota> {
        quotas.get(language)
    }

    on list_quotas() -> Map<String, RuntimeQuota> {
        quotas
    }

    // ── Scaling Policies ───────────────────────────────────────────────

    on add_scaling_policy(policy: ScalingPolicy) -> String {
        let id = generate_policy_id()
        scaling_policies.push(policy.with_id(id))
        id
    }

    on remove_scaling_policy(id: String) -> bool {
        let len = scaling_policies.len()
        scaling_policies = scaling_policies.filter(|p| p.id != id)
        len != scaling_policies.len()
    }

    on list_scaling_policies() -> List<ScalingPolicy> {
        scaling_policies
    }

    // ── Scheduling Logic (runs every minute) ───────────────────────────

    fn start_scheduler_loop() {
        loop {
            sleep_ms(60_000)
            rebalance_resources()
        }
    }

    fn rebalance_resources() {
        let current_load = collect_current_load()
        let desired_quotas = compute_desired_quotas(current_load)

        for (lang, desired) in desired_quotas {
            let current = quotas.get(lang)
            if current == null || desired.cpu_cores != current.cpu_cores || desired.memory_mb != current.memory_mb {
                set_quota(lang, desired)
                audit_log::log("resource_rebalanced", lang, desired)
            }
        }
    }

    fn collect_current_load() -> Map<String, LoadMetric> {
        let all_langs = security.list_installed_packages()
        let mut loads = Map::new()
        for lang in all_langs {
            let stats = perf.get_stats(lang, "titan")
            if stats != null && stats.total_calls > 10 {
                let calls_per_sec = stats.total_calls / ( (now() - stats.first_seen) / 1000 )
                loads.set(lang, LoadMetric {
                    calls_per_sec,
                    avg_latency_us: stats.total_latency_us / stats.total_calls,
                    error_rate: (stats.total_calls - stats.success_calls) as f32 / stats.total_calls as f32,
                })
            }
        }
        loads
    }

    fn compute_desired_quotas(loads: Map<String, LoadMetric>) -> Map<String, RuntimeQuota> {
        let total_calls = loads.values().map(|l| l.calls_per_sec).sum()
        let mut desired = Map::new()
        for (lang, load) in loads {
            let cpu_share = (load.calls_per_sec as f32 / total_calls as f32) * node_capacity.total_cpu_cores
            let memory_share = (load.calls_per_sec as f32 / total_calls as f32) * node_capacity.total_memory_mb
            desired.set(lang, RuntimeQuota {
                cpu_cores: max(1, ceil(cpu_share)),
                memory_mb: max(128, ceil(memory_share)),
                io_weight: if load.error_rate > 0.05 { 1 } else { 10 },
                priority: if load.avg_latency_us < 1000 { 3 } else if load.avg_latency_us < 10000 { 2 } else { 1 },
            })
        }
        // Ensure total doesn't exceed capacity (cap and redistribute)
        let total_cpu = desired.values().map(|q| q.cpu_cores).sum()
        let total_mem = desired.values().map(|q| q.memory_mb).sum()
        if total_cpu > node_capacity.total_cpu_cores {
            let ratio = node_capacity.total_cpu_cores as f32 / total_cpu as f32
            for (lang, quota) in desired {
                quota.cpu_cores = max(1, (quota.cpu_cores as f32 * ratio) as u32)
            }
        }
        if total_mem > node_capacity.total_memory_mb {
            let ratio = node_capacity.total_memory_mb as f32 / total_mem as f32
            for (lang, quota) in desired {
                quota.memory_mb = max(128, (quota.memory_mb as f32 * ratio) as u32)
            }
        }
        desired
    }

    fn apply_quota(lang: String, quota: RuntimeQuota) {
        // Inform the kernel's capability system to enforce the new quota
        kernel_cap::set_process_quota(lang, quota.cpu_cores, quota.memory_mb, quota.io_weight)
        // Update the language runtime's vault limits
        let vault_id = get_vault_for_language(lang)
        if vault_id != null {
            sanctum::set_memory_limit(vault_id, quota.memory_mb * 1024 * 1024)
            sanctum::set_cpu_weight(vault_id, quota.priority)
        }
    }

    // ── Autoscaling ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    fn start_scaler_loop() {
        loop {
            sleep_ms(30_000)   // every 30 seconds
            evaluate_scaling_policies()
        }
    }

    fn evaluate_scaling_policies() {
        let current = collect_current_load()
        for policy in scaling_policies {
            let lang_metric = current.get(policy.language)
            if lang_metric == null { continue }

            let current_replicas = get_current_replicas(policy.language)
            let target_replicas = compute_target_replicas(policy, lang_metric, current_replicas)

            if target_replicas != current_replicas {
                scale_language(policy.language, target_replicas)
                scaling_history.push(ScalingEvent {
                    timestamp: now(),
                    language: policy.language,
                    from_replicas: current_replicas,
                    to_replicas: target_replicas,
                    reason: format!("Policy '{}' triggered (cps={}, error={})", policy.name, lang_metric.calls_per_sec, lang_metric.error_rate),
                })
            }
        }
    }

    fn compute_target_replicas(policy: ScalingPolicy, metric: LoadMetric, current: u32) -> u32 {
        let desired = match policy.metric {
            "calls_per_sec" => ceil(metric.calls_per_sec / policy.target_per_replica)
            "error_rate" => if metric.error_rate > policy.high_threshold { current + 1 }
                           else if metric.error_rate < policy.low_threshold && current > policy.min_replicas { current - 1 }
                           else { current }
            _ => current
        }
        clamp(desired, policy.min_replicas, policy.max_replicas)
    }

    async fn scale_language(lang: String, replicas: u32) {
        let current = get_current_replicas(lang)
        if replicas > current {
            // Scale up
            for i in current..replicas {
                spawn_runtime_vault(lang)
            }
        } else if replicas < current {
            // Scale down – gracefully drain and remove
            let to_remove = current - replicas
            for _ in 0..to_remove {
                drain_and_remove_vault(lang)
            }
        }
    }

    // ── Node Capacity Detection ────────────────────────────────────────

    fn load_node_capacity() {
        node_capacity = NodeCapacity {
            total_cpu_cores: detect_cpu_cores(),
            total_memory_mb: detect_memory_mb(),
            total_io_bandwidth_mb_s: detect_io_bandwidth(),
            available_cpu_cores: node_capacity.total_cpu_cores,
            available_memory_mb: node_capacity.total_memory_mb,
        }
    }

    // ── WebSocket API ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

    fn start_api() {
        websocket.on_message(|msg| {
            match msg.command {
                "set_quota" => {
                    let result = set_quota(msg.language, msg.quota)
                    websocket.reply(result)
                }
                "get_quota" => {
                    let quota = get_quota(msg.language)
                    websocket.reply(quota)
                }
                "list_quotas" => {
                    let quotas = list_quotas()
                    websocket.reply(quotas)
                }
                "add_policy" => {
                    let id = add_scaling_policy(msg.policy)
                    websocket.reply(json({ policy_id: id }))
                }
                "list_policies" => {
                    let policies = list_scaling_policies()
                    websocket.reply(policies)
                }
                "capacity" => {
                    websocket.reply(node_capacity)
                }
                "history" => {
                    websocket.reply(scaling_history)
                }
                _ => websocket.reply(error("Unknown command"))
            }
        })
    }
}

// ── Type Definitions ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

struct RuntimeQuota {
    cpu_cores: u32,
    memory_mb: u32,
    io_weight: u32,
    priority: u32,  // 1-3 (1=background, 3=real‑time)
}

struct NodeCapacity {
    total_cpu_cores: u32,
    total_memory_mb: u32,
    total_io_bandwidth_mb_s: u32,
    available_cpu_cores: u32,
    available_memory_mb: u32,
}

struct LoadMetric {
    calls_per_sec: f32,
    avg_latency_us: u64,
    error_rate: f32,
}

struct ScalingPolicy {
    id: String,
    name: String,
    language: String,
    metric: String,          // "calls_per_sec", "error_rate", "latency"
    target_per_replica: f32, // for calls_per_sec
    high_threshold: f32,     // for error_rate or latency
    low_threshold: f32,
    min_replicas: u32,
    max_replicas: u32,
    cooldown_secs: u64,
}

struct ScalingEvent {
    timestamp: u64,
    language: String,
    from_replicas: u32,
    to_replicas: u32,
    reason: String,
}
```

---

## 2. Sylva CLI for Resource Management (`tools/resource_cli.sv`)

Command‑line interface to view and modify quotas, scaling policies, and capacity.

```sylva
// tools/resource_cli.sv – CLI for Polyglot Resource Scheduler
module polyglot::tools::resource_cli

use polyglot::resource_scheduler::PolyglotResourceScheduler
use core::io::println

let scheduler = PolyglotResourceScheduler::connect("aether://resource-sched")

pub fn main(args: List<String>) {
    if args.is_empty() {
        println("Usage: rs <quota|policy|capacity|history> [options]")
        return
    }
    match args[0] {
        "quota" => cmd_quota(args.tail())
        "policy" => cmd_policy(args.tail())
        "capacity" => cmd_capacity()
        "history" => cmd_history()
        _ => println("Unknown command")
    }
}

fn cmd_quota(args: List<String>) {
    let subcmd = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    match subcmd {
        "set" => {
            let lang = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            let cpu = args.get(2).unwrap_or("0").parse_u32().unwrap_or(0)
            let mem = args.get(3).unwrap_or("0").parse_u32().unwrap_or(0)
            if lang.is_empty() || cpu == 0 || mem == 0 {
                println("Usage: rs quota set <lang> <cpu_cores> <memory_mb>")
                return
            }
            match scheduler.set_quota(lang, cpu, mem) {
                Ok(()) => println("Quota set.")
                Err(e) => println("Error: " + e)
            }
        }
        "get" => {
            let lang = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            let quota = scheduler.get_quota(lang)
            match quota {
                Some(q) => println(format!("{} | CPU:{} cores | MEM:{} MB", lang, q.cpu_cores, q.memory_mb))
                None => println("No quota set for " + lang)
            }
        }
        "list" => {
            let quotas = scheduler.list_quotas()
            if quotas.is_empty() {
                println("No quotas set (default unlimited).")
                return
            }
            println("Current Quotas:")
            for (lang, q) in quotas {
                println(format!("  {} | CPU:{} cores | MEM:{} MB", lang, q.cpu_cores, q.memory_mb))
            }
        }
        _ => println("Usage: rs quota set|get|list")
    }
}

fn cmd_policy(args: List<String>) {
    let subcmd = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    match subcmd {
        "add" => {
            let name = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            let lang = args.get(2).unwrap_or("")
            let metric = args.get(3).unwrap_or("calls_per_sec")
            let target = args.get(4).unwrap_or("").parse_f32().unwrap_or(100.0)
            let min = args.get(5).unwrap_or("1").parse_u32().unwrap_or(1)
            let max = args.get(6).unwrap_or("10").parse_u32().unwrap_or(10)
            let id = scheduler.add_policy(name, lang, metric, target, min, max)
            println("Policy added. ID: " + id)
        }
        "remove" => {
            let id = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            if scheduler.remove_policy(id) {
                println("Policy removed.")
            } else {
                println("Policy not found.")
            }
        }
        "list" => {
            let policies = scheduler.list_policies()
            for p in policies {
                println(format!("{} | {} | {} | target={} | replicas={}-{}", p.id, p.name, p.language, p.target_per_replica, p.min_replicas, p.max_replicas))
            }
        }
        _ => println("Usage: rs policy add|remove|list")
    }
}

fn cmd_capacity() {
    let cap = scheduler.get_capacity()
    println(format!("CPU cores: {}/{}", cap.available_cpu_cores, cap.total_cpu_cores))
    println(format!("Memory: {}/{} MB", cap.available_memory_mb, cap.total_memory_mb))
    println(format!("I/O bandwidth: {} MB/s", cap.total_io_bandwidth_mb_s))
}

fn cmd_history() {
    let events = scheduler.get_history()
    if events.is_empty() {
        println("No scaling events.")
        return
    }
    println("Scaling History:")
    for ev in events {
        println(format!("  {} | {} -> {} replicas | {}", ev.timestamp, ev.from_replicas, ev.to_replicas, ev.reason))
    }
}
```

- **Connections Router** routes calls to scaled‑up replicas (via load balancing).

rs quota set rust 4 2048

# Add scaling policy for Python (scale based on calls per second)
rs policy add "python_scaler" python calls_per_sec 500 2 10

# Check current capacity
rs capacity
# Output: CPU cores: 6/8, Memory: 4096/8192 MB

# View scaling history
rs history

## 5. Conclusion

The Polyglot Resource Scheduler & Autoscaler completes the Omnisystem's polyglot infrastructure by ensuring that every language runtime gets fair and efficient resource allocation. It automatically adjusts quotas based on real‑time load, scales language‑specific connector pools up or down, and respects global node capacity. Combined with the CI/CD pipeline, workflows, debugging, and security, the system now provides a fully managed, production‑grade environment for developing and running polyglot applications at scale. 🚀", "The Polyglot Resource Scheduler & Autoscaler is now fully implemented, providing dynamic resource allocation, quota enforcement, and automatic scaling for all language runtimes. The Aether actor monitors real‑time load, adjusts CPU/memory limits, and scales connector pools up or down based on configurable policies. A Sylva CLI and a minimal web dashboard give operators full visibility and control.

```aether
// services/resource_scheduler.ae – Polyglot Resource Scheduler & Autoscaler
actor PolyglotResourceScheduler {
    var perf: PerformanceAnalyzer
    var security: PolyglotSecurityManager
    var router: ConnectionsRouter
    var sanctum: SanctumManager
    var quotas: Map<String, RuntimeQuota> = empty()
    var node_capacity: NodeCapacity
    var scaling_policies: List<ScalingPolicy> = empty()
    var scaling_history: List<ScalingEvent> = empty()
    var websocket: WebSocketServer

    on new(perf_addr: String, security_addr: String, router_addr: String, sanctum_addr: String, ws_port: u16) {
        perf = PerformanceAnalyzer::connect(perf_addr)
        security = PolyglotSecurityManager::connect(security_addr)
        router = ConnectionsRouter::connect(router_addr)
        sanctum = SanctumManager::connect(sanctum_addr)
        websocket = WebSocketServer::bind(ws_port)
        load_node_capacity()
        load_quotas()
        start_scheduler_loop()
        start_scaler_loop()
    }

    // ── Quota Management ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    on set_quota(language: String, quota: RuntimeQuota) -> Result<(), String> {
        if !validate_quota(quota) { return Err("Invalid quota (exceeds node capacity)") }
        quotas.set(language, quota)
        apply_quota(language, quota)
        audit_log::log("quota_set", language, quota)
        Ok(())
    }

    on get_quota(language: String) -> Option<RuntimeQuota> {
        quotas.get(language)
    }

    on list_quotas() -> Map<String, RuntimeQuota> {
        quotas
    }

    // ── Scaling Policies ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    on add_scaling_policy(policy: ScalingPolicy) -> String {
        let id = generate_policy_id()
        scaling_policies.push(policy.with_id(id))
        id
    }

    on remove_scaling_policy(id: String) -> bool {
        let len = scaling_policies.len()
        scaling_policies = scaling_policies.filter(|p| p.id != id)
        len != scaling_policies.len()
    }

    on list_scaling_policies() -> List<ScalingPolicy> {
        scaling_policies
    }

    // ── Scheduling Logic ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    fn start_scheduler_loop() {
        loop {
            sleep_ms(60_000)
            rebalance_resources()
        }
    }

    fn rebalance_resources() {
        let current_load = collect_current_load()
        let desired = compute_desired_quotas(current_load)
        for (lang, quota) in desired {
            let old = quotas.get(lang)
            if old == null || quota.cpu_cores != old.cpu_cores || quota.memory_mb != old.memory_mb {
                set_quota(lang, quota).ok()
                audit_log::log("resource_rebalanced", lang, quota)
            }
        }
    }

    fn collect_current_load() -> Map<String, LoadMetric> {
        let all_langs = security.list_installed_packages()
        let mut loads = Map::new()
        for lang in all_langs {
            let stats = perf.get_stats(lang, "titan")
            if stats != null && stats.total_calls > 10 {
                let elapsed = (now() - stats.first_seen).max(1)
                let calls_per_sec = stats.total_calls as f32 / (elapsed / 1000) as f32
                loads.set(lang, LoadMetric {
                    calls_per_sec,
                    avg_latency_us: stats.total_latency_us / stats.total_calls,
                    error_rate: (stats.total_calls - stats.success_calls) as f32 / stats.total_calls as f32,
                })
            }
        }
        loads
    }

    fn compute_desired_quotas(loads: Map<String, LoadMetric>) -> Map<String, RuntimeQuota> {
        let total_calls = loads.values().map(|l| l.calls_per_sec).sum()
        if total_calls == 0.0 { return Map::new() }
        let mut desired = Map::new()
        for (lang, load) in loads {
            let share = load.calls_per_sec / total_calls
            let cpu = (share * node_capacity.total_cpu_cores as f32).ceil() as u32
            let mem = (share * node_capacity.total_memory_mb as f32).ceil() as u32
            desired.set(lang, RuntimeQuota {
                cpu_cores: cpu.max(1),
                memory_mb: mem.max(128),
                io_weight: if load.error_rate > 0.05 { 1 } else { 10 },
                priority: if load.avg_latency_us < 1000 { 3 } else if load.avg_latency_us < 10000 { 2 } else { 1 },
            })
        }
        // Cap totals to node capacity
        let total_cpu: u32 = desired.values().map(|q| q.cpu_cores).sum()
        let total_mem: u32 = desired.values().map(|q| q.memory_mb).sum()
        if total_cpu > node_capacity.total_cpu_cores {
            let ratio = node_capacity.total_cpu_cores as f32 / total_cpu as f32
            for (_, quota) in desired {
                quota.cpu_cores = (quota.cpu_cores as f32 * ratio).ceil() as u32
            }
        }
        if total_mem > node_capacity.total_memory_mb {
            let ratio = node_capacity.total_memory_mb as f32 / total_mem as f32
            for (_, quota) in desired {
                quota.memory_mb = (quota.memory_mb as f32 * ratio).ceil() as u32
            }
        }
        desired
    }

    fn apply_quota(lang: String, quota: RuntimeQuota) {
        kernel_cap::set_process_quota(lang, quota.cpu_cores, quota.memory_mb, quota.io_weight)
        let vault_id = get_vault_for_language(lang)
        if vault_id != null {
            sanctum.set_memory_limit(vault_id, quota.memory_mb * 1024 * 1024)
            sanctum.set_cpu_weight(vault_id, quota.priority)
        }
    }

    // ── Autoscaling ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    fn start_scaler_loop() {
        loop {
            sleep_ms(30_000)
            evaluate_scaling_policies()
        }
    }

    fn evaluate_scaling_policies() {
        let current = collect_current_load()
        for policy in scaling_policies {
            let metric = current.get(policy.language)
            if metric == null { continue }
            let current_rep = get_current_replicas(policy.language)
            let target_rep = compute_target_replicas(policy, metric, current_rep)
            if target_rep != current_rep {
                scale_language(policy.language, target_rep)
                scaling_history.push(ScalingEvent {
                    timestamp: now(),
                    language: policy.language,
                    from_replicas: current_rep,
                    to_replicas: target_rep,
                    reason: format("Policy '{}'", policy.name),
                })
            }
        }
    }

    fn compute_target_replicas(policy: ScalingPolicy, metric: LoadMetric, current: u32) -> u32 {
        let desired = match policy.metric {
            "calls_per_sec" => (metric.calls_per_sec / policy.target_per_replica).ceil() as u32,
            "error_rate" => if metric.error_rate > policy.high_threshold { current + 1 }
                            else if metric.error_rate < policy.low_threshold && current > policy.min_replicas { current - 1 }
                            else { current },
            _ => current
        }
        desired.clamp(policy.min_replicas, policy.max_replicas)
    }

    async fn scale_language(lang: String, replicas: u32) {
        let current = get_current_replicas(lang)
        if replicas > current {
            for _ in current..replicas { spawn_runtime_vault(lang) }
        } else if replicas < current {
            for _ in 0..(current - replicas) { drain_and_remove_vault(lang) }
        }
    }

    // ── Node Capacity ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    fn load_node_capacity() {
        node_capacity = NodeCapacity {
            total_cpu_cores: detect_cpu_cores(),
            total_memory_mb: detect_memory_mb(),
            total_io_bandwidth_mb_s: detect_io_bandwidth(),
            available_cpu_cores: 0,
            available_memory_mb: 0,
        }
    }

    // ── WebSocket API ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    fn start_api() {
        websocket.on_message(|msg| {
            match msg.command {
                "set_quota" => { websocket.reply(set_quota(msg.language, msg.quota)) }
                "get_quota" => { websocket.reply(get_quota(msg.language)) }
                "list_quotas" => { websocket.reply(list_quotas()) }
                "add_policy" => { websocket.reply(add_scaling_policy(msg.policy)) }
                "remove_policy" => { websocket.reply(remove_scaling_policy(msg.id)) }
                "list_policies" => { websocket.reply(list_scaling_policies()) }
                "capacity" => { websocket.reply(node_capacity) }
                "history" => { websocket.reply(scaling_history) }
                _ => websocket.reply(error("Unknown command"))
            }
        })
    }
}

struct RuntimeQuota {
    cpu_cores: u32,
    memory_mb: u32,
    io_weight: u32,
    priority: u32,
}

struct NodeCapacity {
    total_cpu_cores: u32,
    total_memory_mb: u32,
    total_io_bandwidth_mb_s: u32,
    available_cpu_cores: u32,
    available_memory_mb: u32,
}

struct LoadMetric {
    calls_per_sec: f32,
    avg_latency_us: u64,
    error_rate: f32,
}

struct ScalingPolicy {
    id: String,
    name: String,
    language: String,
    metric: String,
    target_per_replica: f32,
    high_threshold: f32,
    low_threshold: f32,
    min_replicas: u32,
    max_replicas: u32,
    cooldown_secs: u64,
}

struct ScalingEvent {
    timestamp: u64,
    language: String,
    from_replicas: u32,
    to_replicas: u32,
    reason: String,
}
```

```sylva
// tools/resource_cli.sv – CLI for Polyglot Resource Scheduler
module polyglot::tools::resource_cli

use polyglot::resource_scheduler::PolyglotResourceScheduler
use core::io::println

let scheduler = PolyglotResourceScheduler::connect("aether://resource-sched")

pub fn main(args: List<String>) {
    if args.is_empty() {
        println("Usage: rs <quota|policy|capacity|history> [options]")
        return
    }
    match args[0] {
        "quota" => cmd_quota(args.tail())
        "policy" => cmd_policy(args.tail())
        "capacity" => cmd_capacity()
        "history" => cmd_history()
        _ => println("Unknown command")
    }
}

fn cmd_quota(args: List<String>) {
    let subcmd = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    match subcmd {
        "set" => {
            let lang = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            let cpu = args.get(2).unwrap_or("0").parse_u32().unwrap_or(0)
            let mem = args.get(3).unwrap_or("0").parse_u32().unwrap_or(0)
            if lang.is_empty() || cpu == 0 || mem == 0 {
                println("Usage: rs quota set <lang> <cpu_cores> <memory_mb>")
                return
            }
            let quota = RuntimeQuota { cpu_cores: cpu, memory_mb: mem, io_weight: 10, priority: 2 }
            match scheduler.set_quota(lang, quota) {
                Ok(()) => println("Quota set for " + lang),
                Err(e) => println("Error: " + e),
            }
        }
        "get" => {
            let lang = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            let quota = scheduler.get_quota(lang)
            match quota {
                Some(q) => println(format("{} | CPU: {} cores | MEM: {} MB", lang, q.cpu_cores, q.memory_mb)),
                None => println("No quota set for " + lang),
            }
        }
        "list" => {
            let quotas = scheduler.list_quotas()
            if quotas.is_empty() { println("No quotas defined."); return }
            println("Current Quotas:")
            for (lang, q) in quotas {
                println(format("  {} | CPU: {} cores | MEM: {} MB", lang, q.cpu_cores, q.memory_mb))
            }
        }
        _ => println("Usage: rs quota set|get|list")
    }
}

fn cmd_policy(args: List<String>) {
    let subcmd = args.get(0).unwrap_or("")
    match subcmd {
        "add" => {
            let name = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            let lang = args.get(2).unwrap_or("")
            let metric = args.get(3).unwrap_or("calls_per_sec")
            let target = args.get(4).unwrap_or("100").parse_f32().unwrap_or(100.0)
            let min = args.get(5).unwrap_or("1").parse_u32().unwrap_or(1)
            let max = args.get(6).unwrap_or("10").parse_u32().unwrap_or(10)
            let policy = ScalingPolicy {
                name, language: lang, metric, target_per_replica: target,
                high_threshold: 0.0, low_threshold: 0.0, min_replicas: min, max_replicas: max,
                cooldown_secs: 60,
            }
            let id = scheduler.add_scaling_policy(policy)
            println("Policy added. ID: " + id)
        }
        "remove" => {
            let id = args.get(1).unwrap_or("")
            if scheduler.remove_scaling_policy(id) {
                println("Policy removed.")
            } else {
                println("Policy not found.")
            }
        }
        "list" => {
            let policies = scheduler.list_scaling_policies()
            for p in policies {
                println(format("{} | {} | {} | target={} | min={} max={}", p.id, p.name, p.language, p.target_per_replica, p.min_replicas, p.max_replicas))
            }
        }
        _ => println("Usage: rs policy add|remove|list")
    }
}

fn cmd_capacity() {
    let cap = scheduler.get_capacity()
    println(format("CPU: {}/{} cores", cap.available_cpu_cores, cap.total_cpu_cores))
    println(format("Memory: {}/{} MB", cap.available_memory_mb, cap.total_memory_mb))
    println(format("I/O Bandwidth: {} MB/s", cap.total_io_bandwidth_mb_s))
}

fn cmd_history() {
    let events = scheduler.get_history()
    if events.is_empty() {
        println("No scaling events recorded.")
        return
    }
    println("Scaling History:")
    for ev in events {
        println(format("  {} | {} → {} replicas | {}", ev.timestamp, ev.from_replicas, ev.to_replicas, ev.reason))
    }
}
```

Update the master deployment script:
